    1 $accept: Program EOF
             ;

    2 Program: PDeclaration Program
    3        | EOF
             ;

    4 PDeclaration: EventDecl
    5             | MachineDecl
                  ;

    6 Type: T_INT
    7     | T_BOOL
    8     | T_EVENTID
    9     | T_MACHINEID
   10     | T_ANY
   11     | NamedTupleType
   12     | TupleType
   13     | SeqType
          ;

   14 NamedTupleType: LPAREN FieldTypeList RPAREN
                    ;

   15 FieldTypeList: ID COLON Type
   16              | FieldTypeList COMMA ID COLON Type
                   ;

   17 TupleType: LPAREN TypeList RPAREN
               ;

   18 TypeList: Type
   19         | Type COMMA TypeList
              ;

   20 SeqType: T_SEQ LBRACKET Type RBRACKET
             ;

   21 EventDecl: EVENT ID TypeOrNull AnnotationOrNull SEMICOLON
               ;

   22 AnnotationOrNull: ASSERT INT
   23                 | ASSUME INT
   24                 | /* empty */
                      ;

   25 TypeOrNull: COLON Type
   26           | /* empty */
                ;

   27 MachineDecl: IsMain IsGhost MACHINE ID LCBRACE MachineBody RCBRACE
                 ;

   28 IsGhost: GHOST
   29        | /* empty */
             ;

   30 IsMain: MAIN
   31       | /* empty */
            ;

   32 MachineBody: /* empty */
   33            | MachineBodyItem MachineBody
                 ;

   34 MachineBodyItem: VarDecl
   35                | StateDecl
   36                | ActionDecl
   37                | FunDecl
   38                | MaxQueueSizeDecl
   39                | SubmachineDecl
                     ;

   40 SubmachineDecl: SUBMACHINE ID LCBRACE SubmachineBody RCBRACE
                    ;

   41 SubmachineBody: StateDecl SubmachineBody
   42               | /* empty */
                    ;

   43 MaxQueueSizeDecl: MAXQUEUE INT SEMICOLON
                      ;

   44 VarList: ID
   45        | ID COMMA VarList
             ;

   46 VarDecl: IsGhost VAR VarList COLON Type SEMICOLON
             ;

   47 FunDecl: IsForeign FUN AttributeOrNull ID Params TypeOrNull StmtBlock
             ;

   48 Params: LPAREN RPAREN
   49       | NamedTupleType
            ;

   50 IsForeign: FOREIGN
   51          | /* empty */
               ;

   52 ActionDecl: ACTION ID StmtBlock
                ;

   53 StateDecl: StartOrNull STATE ID LCBRACE StateBody RCBRACE
               ;

   54 StartOrNull: START
   55            | /* empty */
                 ;

   56 StateBody: /* empty */
   57          | StateBodyItem StateBody
               ;

   58 NonDefaultEventList: ID
   59                    | ID COMMA EventList
                         ;

   60 EventList: EventID
   61          | EventID COMMA EventList
               ;

   62 EventID: ID
   63        | DEFAULT
             ;

   64 StateBodyItem: ENTRY StmtBlock
   65              | EXIT StmtBlock
   66              | DEFER NonDefaultEventList SEMICOLON
   67              | IGNORE NonDefaultEventList SEMICOLON
   68              | ON EventList GOTO ID SEMICOLON
   69              | ON EventList PUSH ID SEMICOLON
   70              | ON EventList DO ID SEMICOLON
                   ;

   71 Stmt: IF Exp Stmt ELSE Stmt
   72     | IF Exp Stmt
   73     | WHILE Exp Stmt
   74     | Exp ASSIGN Exp SEMICOLON
   75     | StmtBlock
   76     | ASSERT LPAREN Exp RPAREN SEMICOLON
   77     | SEND LPAREN Exp COMMA Exp OptionalLastArg RPAREN SEMICOLON
   78     | SCALL LPAREN Exp RPAREN SEMICOLON
   79     | RAISE LPAREN Exp OptionalLastArg RPAREN SEMICOLON
   80     | FFCall SEMICOLON
   81     | RETURN ExpOrNull SEMICOLON
   82     | LEAVE SEMICOLON
   83     | SEMICOLON
   84     | DELETE SEMICOLON
   85     | Exp Args SEMICOLON
          ;

   86 OptionalLastArg: COMMA Exp
   87                | /* empty */
                     ;

   88 StmtList: /* empty */
   89         | StmtList Stmt
              ;

   90 StmtBlock: LCBRACE StmtList RCBRACE
               ;

   91 Unary: MINUS
   92      | LNOT
           ;

   93 Multiplicative: MUL
   94               | DIV
                    ;

   95 Additive: PLUS
   96         | MINUS
              ;

   97 Relational: LT
   98           | GT
   99           | LE
  100           | GE
                ;

  101 Equality: EQ
  102         | NE
              ;

  103 Exp: Exp_8
         ;

  104 Exp_8: Exp_8 LOR Exp_7
  105      | Exp_7
           ;

  106 Exp_7: Exp_7 LAND Exp_6
  107      | Exp_6
           ;

  108 Exp_6: MUL
  109      | Exp_5
           ;

  110 Exp_5: Exp_4 Equality Exp_4
  111      | Exp_4
           ;

  112 Exp_4: Exp_3 Relational Exp_3
  113      | Exp_3
           ;

  114 Exp_3: Exp_3 Additive Exp_2
  115      | Exp_2
           ;

  116 Exp_2: Exp_2 Multiplicative Exp_1
  117      | Exp_1
           ;

  118 Exp_1: Unary Exp_0
  119      | Exp_0
           ;

  120 Exp_0: Exp_0 DOT ID
  121      | Exp_0 LBRACKET Exp RBRACKET
  122      | BaseId
  123      | INT
  124      | Bool
  125      | NamedTuple
  126      | Tuple
  127      | LPAREN Exp RPAREN
  128      | NewExp
  129      | Arg
  130      | FFCall
  131      | SIZEOF LPAREN Exp RPAREN
           ;

  132 Arg: LPAREN Type RPAREN PayloadKw
  133    | PayloadKw
         ;

  134 PayloadKw: PAYLOAD
  135          | ARG
               ;

  136 ExpList: Exp
  137        | ExpList COMMA Exp
             ;

  138 Tuple: LPAREN Exp COMMA RPAREN
  139      | LPAREN Exp COMMA ExpList RPAREN
           ;

  140 NamedExpList: ID ASSIGN Exp
  141             | ID ASSIGN Exp COMMA NamedExpList
                  ;

  142 NamedTuple: LPAREN NamedExpList RPAREN
                ;

  143 ExpOrNull: Exp
  144          | /* empty */
               ;

  145 NewExp: NEW ID KWArgs
            ;

  146 Bool: TRUE
  147     | FALSE
          ;

  148 FFCall: ID Args
            ;

  149 KWArgList: ID ASSIGN Exp
  150          | ID ASSIGN Exp COMMA KWArgList
               ;

  151 KWArgs: LPAREN KWArgList RPAREN
  152       | LPAREN RPAREN
            ;

  153 Args: LPAREN ArgList RPAREN
  154     | LPAREN RPAREN
          ;

  156        | Exp COMMA ArgList
             ;

  157 BaseId: ID
  158       | THIS
  159       | TRIGGER
  160       | DEFAULT
  161       | NULL
            ;

  162 Attribute: LCBRACE ID RCBRACE
               ;

  163 AttributeOrNull: Attribute
  164                | /* empty */
                     ;
